### [329] [A comprehensive study on ILP acceleration accounting for sparsity, area, energy, data movement using near-memory architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17158)
*Siddhartha Raman Sundara Raman,Lizy K John,Jaydeep P. Kulkarni*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出SPARK，一种利用现有CPU L1缓存进行近缓存加速的ILP加速器，通过稀疏感知和重用感知架构，在极低硬件开销下实现相比CPU最高15倍性能提升和152倍能耗降低，相比GPU最高20倍性能提升和740倍能耗降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ILP算法稀疏且分支密集，在传统CPU和GPU上效率低下，大规模ILP问题需要数小时执行时间，限制了其在时间敏感决策场景中的应用。现有CPU求解器（如Gurobi）存在吞吐量瓶颈，GPU求解器则面临线程发散、流多处理器利用不足和频繁的主机-设备交互等问题。

Method: SPARK复用了CPU中现有的L1缓存，以约1.4%的CPU面积开销实现近缓存加速。架构包括：（1）近缓存稀疏检测和稀疏感知计算，减少无关计算和数据移动能耗；（2）利用ILP算法中的计算重用模式提升并行度和效率；（3）支持稀疏和稠密ILP以及线性规划（LP）。

Result: 基于MIPLIB 2017真实工作负载评估：稀疏ILP相比AMD Zen3 CPU实现最高15倍性能提升和152倍能耗降低，相比NVIDIA Tesla V100 GPU实现最高20倍性能提升和740倍能耗降低；稀疏LP实现7-17倍性能提升和103-250倍能耗降低。

Conclusion: SPARK通过硬件-算法协同设计，以极小硬件开销显著加速ILP/LP求解，验证了近缓存架构在稀疏优化问题领域的广泛适用性，为时间敏感的决策优化任务提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Integer Linear Programming (ILP) is widely used for solving real-world optimization problems, including network routing, map routing, and traffic scheduling. However, ILP algorithms are sparse and branch-intensive, making them inefficient on conventional CPUs and GPUs. Prior work has shown that large-scale ILP problems can require tens of hours of execution time even on massively parallel systems, limiting their applicability to time-sensitive decision-making workloads. Existing ILP solvers such as Gurobi employ software-level optimizations to handle sparsity on CPUs, but still face throughput limitations. GPU-based ILP solvers are also constrained because GPUs are not well suited for sparse and branch-heavy workloads, leading to thread divergence, under-utilization of streaming multiprocessors, and frequent host-device interactions.
  This paper presents SPARK, a sparsity-aware, reuse-aware, energy-efficient, reconfigurable near-cache ILP accelerator. SPARK repurposes the existing L1 cache in CPUs to provide near-cache acceleration with minimal hardware overhead of approximately 1.4\% of the CPU area. The architecture performs near-cache sparsity detection and sparsity-aware computation to reduce insignificant computations and data movement energy. SPARK also exploits computational reuse patterns in ILP algorithms to improve parallelism and efficiency. The proposed design supports both sparse and dense ILPs as well as Linear Programs (LPs).
  Evaluations on real-world workloads from MIPLIB 2017 show that SPARK achieves up to 15x and 20x performance improvement, and up to 152x and 740x energy reduction compared to AMD Zen3 CPUs and NVIDIA Tesla V100 GPUs, respectively, for sparse ILPs. For sparse LPs, SPARK achieves 7-17x performance improvement and 103-250x energy reduction over CPU and GPU baselines, demonstrating the broad applicability of the proposed architecture.

### [330] [Workload-Aware Early-Stage Power Delivery Network Optimization via Architectural Power Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17182)
*Oran Hayes,Maria Pantazi-Kypraiou,Athanasios Tziouvaras,George Stamoulis,Anuj Pathania,Shreejith Shanker,George Floros*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Power Delivery Networks (PDNs) are critical for maintaining voltage integrity in modern multiprocessor systems. This paper proposes a workload-aware methodology for early-stage PDN optimization based on architectural power traces. Using architectural simulations, temporal power activity is captured at fine granularity and mapped to spatial power density distributions across the chip. These distributions are then translated into current demand profiles to guide PDN topology planning at tile granularity. By incorporating realistic workload behavior, the proposed approach enables adaptive PDN resource allocation during early design stages. ### [331] [VeriCache: Turning Lossy KV Cache into Lossless LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17613)
*Jiayi Yao,Samuel Shen,Kuntai Du,Shaoting Feng,Dongjoo Seo,Rui Zhang,Yuyang Huang,Yuhan Liu,Shan Lu,Junchen Jiang*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: VeriCache 是一个推理框架，通过压缩KV缓存进行草稿解码，再使用完整KV缓存验证来保证输出一致性，同时保持高吞吐量，最高可达4X加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存压缩方法虽然能提升吞吐量，但都是有损的——随着解码更多token，输出会逐渐偏离完整KV缓存的输出，导致代码生成和工具调用等场景出现灾难性失败。

Method: 使用压缩KV缓存草稿token，再用完整KV缓存验证；利用压缩KV解码（HBM带宽受限）与完整KV缓存加载（PCIe/网络受限）的并行性，以及草稿相似性实现长草稿视野以摊销交换开销。

Result: 相比完整KV推理，VeriCache实现高达4倍的吞吐量提升，同时输出完全相同。

Conclusion: VeriCache成功将无损保证与高吞吐量结合，统一支持多种压缩方法，并可与传统投机解码组合使用。

Abstract: The large size of the KV cache has become a major bottleneck for serving LLMs with increasing context lengths. In response, many KV cache compression methods, such as token dropping and quantization, have been proposed. However, almost all of these methods are inherently lossy-despite minimal accuracy degradation for short outputs, their outputs increasingly diverge from full-KV-cache outputs as more tokens are decoded, which leads to catastrophic failures in code generation and tool calling.
  We present VeriCache, the first inference framework that ensures the same output as full-KV-cache decoding but largely preserves the high decoding throughput of a range of KV cache compression algorithms. VeriCache uses the compressed KV cache to draft tokens, then verifies them against the full KV cache. While it may seem like just speculative decoding, VeriCache requires addressing a key system challenge to work-keeping the full KV cache out of GPU memory and minimizing the overhead of swapping it in for verification. The insight is two-fold: (1) compressed-KV decoding can be parallelized with full-KV swap, because one is HBM-bandwidth-bound and the other is PCIe/network-bound, and (2) the compressed KV cache often produces output similar to the full KV cache, allowing a long drafting horizon to amortize each full-KV swap.
  VeriCache applies to both long-context decoding and remote prefix caching, supports a broad family of token-dropping and quantization methods through a uniform compressor interface, and composes with traditional speculative decoding. Experimental results show that VeriCache achieves up to 4X higher throughput than full-KV inference while producing identical outputs.

</details>


### [332] [μ-ORCA: Optimizing Acceleration for Microsecond-Scale Deep Neural Network Inference on ACAP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17683)
*Shixin Ji,Jinming Zhuang,Zhuoping Yang,Xingzhen Chen,Wei Zhang,Peipei Zhou*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: μ-ORCA是一个面向超低延迟（微秒级）DNN推理的异构加速器框架，通过在AMD ACAP平台上实现AIE阵列间的直接层间通信、512位/周期级联连接以及开销感知的性能模型，成功将6层DeepSets模型的推理延迟降至0.93μs，满足高能物理喷注标记场景的1μs延迟预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异构可重构平台（如AMD ACAP）虽适合DNN推理，但在微秒级小规模问题上存在片上通信效率低、层间延迟大等问题，导致高能物理喷注标记等应用无法满足1μs的延迟预算。此外，硬件开销（如同步、VLIW处理器序言）常被忽视，难以正确优化加速器。

Method: 1) 在AIE阵列上实现DNN层间的直接层间通信，替代共享内存块或FPGA逻辑；2) 采用512位/周期级联连接替代32位/周期的DMA连接；3) 提出开销感知性能模型，适配不同NN层大小，进行设计空间探索优化端到端延迟；4) 支持MLP和DeepSets模型及非矩阵乘内核（bias、ReLU、全局聚合）。

Result: 在AMD ACAP VEK280平台上，μ-ORCA相比最先进的ACAP框架平均延迟降低>1.70倍和>1.83倍；6层真实DeepSets模型延迟达0.93μs，满足延迟预算。

Conclusion: μ-ORCA证明了通过定制化异构加速器框架和开销感知优化，能够使ACAP平台满足微秒级DNN推理的严格延迟要求，为高能物理等实时应用提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Heterogeneous reconfigurable platforms with tensor cores, such as AMD ACAP, are increasingly adopted for deep neural network (DNN) inference due to their high throughput and flexibility. However, their suitability for microsecond-scale inference on small problem sizes remains underexplored. In jet-tagging applications in high-energy physics, inefficient on-chip communication and large inter-layer latency prevent existing frameworks from meeting the 1-μs latency budget. Moreover, hardware overheads such as synchronization and VLIW processor prologue are often overlooked, making it infeasible to optimize accelerators correctly. To address these problems, we propose μ-ORCA, a customized heterogeneous accelerator framework for ultra-low-latency model inference. μ-ORCA enables direct inter-layer communication between DNN layers on the AIE array, instead of using shared memory tiles or FPGA fabric. Moreover, a 512-bit/cycle cascade connection is applied instead of a 32-bit/cycle DMA connection. μ-ORCA also provides an overhead-aware performance model that adapts to different NN layer sizes, and conducts design space exploration to optimize end-to-end latency. μ-ORCA supports MLP and DeepSets models with non-MM kernels, including bias, ReLU, and global aggregation on AIE. We evaluate μ-ORCA on the AMD ACAP VEK280 platform. Experimental results show that μ-ORCA achieves average latency reduction of >1.70$\times$ and >1.83$\times$ compared with different state-of-the-art ACAP frameworks, and achieves 0.93 μs latency for a 6-layer real-world DeepSets model, satisfying the latency budget. We open source μ-ORCA at https://github.com/arc-research-lab/u-ORCA.

</details>


### [333] [ROA-Based Subharmonic Injection Locking for Oscillator-Based Ising Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17720)
*Nicholas Sica,Baris Taskin*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于片上集成旋转行波振荡器（RTWO）的旋转振荡器阵列（ROA）砖块结构，用于在基于振荡器的伊辛机（OIM）中实现稳定的次谐波注入锁定（SHIL），在PVT变化下保持93%-97%的精度，能量消耗为2.49 nJ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在芯片上实现次谐波注入锁定（SHIL）面临挑战，因为SHIL频率需是OIM节点工作频率的整数倍，且片上变化会影响相位、降低SHIL性能，阻碍了OIM实现的可扩展性。

Method: 采用片上集成的旋转行波振荡器（RTWOs）组成旋转振荡器阵列（ROA）砖块结构，生成高频信号作为外部扰动，在基于振荡器的伊辛机（OIM）中诱导次谐波注入锁定（SHIL）。

Result: ROA砖块在PVT变化下提供稳定的2.31 GHz SHIL信号；相比分布式环形振荡器SHIL（ROSC-SHIL）在PVT下完全失效，ROA-SHIL保持93%-97%的精度（与理想SHIL信号相同）；能量消耗为2.49 nJ。

Conclusion: ROA砖块结构能有效克服片上变化对SHIL的不利影响，在PVT变化下保持高精度，且具有良好的可扩展性，为OIM的大规模芯片实现提供了可行方案。

Abstract: This paper introduces on-chip integrated rotary traveling wave oscillators (RTWOs) organized into rotary oscillator array (ROA) bricks as an external perturbation to induce subharmonic injection locking (SHIL) in oscillator-based Ising machines (OIMs). The implementation of SHILs on chip is challenging, as the frequency of SHILs must be multiples of the operating frequency of the OIM nodes, with on-chip variations affecting the phase, degrading the SHIL process. This impedes the scaling of OIM implementations, regardless of the topology of Ising nodes, coupling or graph mapping mechanisms. The ROA brick topology implementation of RTWOs generates high frequency signals that are shown to provide a stable 2.31 GHz SHIL signal under process, voltage, and temperature (PVT) variations. Under PVT variations, distributed ring oscillator-based SHILs (ROSC-SHIL) fail to perform injection locking while the proposed ROA brick-based SHIL (ROA-SHIL) preserve 93% to 97% accuracy (the same accuracy of an ideal SHIL signal) in the OIM solutions of a sample 324-node max-cut problem. The driving strength and floorplan of the ROA brick are also shown to be amenable for scaling with an energy-to-solution impact of 2.49 nJ for the proposed ROA-SHIL.

</details>


### [334] [CPPL: A Circuit Prompt Programming Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17892)
*Shuo Yin,Yihe Wang,Lancheng Zou,Xufeng Yao,Tinghuan Chen,Chen Bai,Zhengrong Wang,Tsung-Yi Ho,Bei Yu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出CPPL框架，通过Python前端DSL和JSON中间表示，将LLM辅助的硬件生成转化为可静态检查的编译前端问题，相比直接生成Verilog或CIRCT IR，显著提升了功能正确性，并能利用CIRCT进行后端优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接让LLM生成RTL代码难以验证、优化和集成到基于编译器的硬件设计流程中；LLM生成原生编译器IR（如MLIR/CIRCT）则面临语法复杂、SSA约束、方言特定操作和严格位宽限制等挑战。

Method: 提出CPPL框架，包含：(1) Python前端DSL，用于声明模块接口和层级；(2) CPPL IR，一种面向LLM友好的JSON格式电路中间表示；(3) 编译器自动推断操作位宽、验证IR合法性、检查层级和端口绑定，并确定性地下译到CIRCT以生成可综合Verilog。

Result: 在RTLLM基准测试上，CPPL相比直接生成Verilog和直接生成CIRCT IR，功能正确性均有提升；经CIRCT优化后，综合后的AIG节点数量减少。

Conclusion: 编译器中介的接口（CPPL）能使LLM辅助的硬件设计更可靠、更可分析，并更有利于后端优化。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in register-transfer level (RTL) design automation, but direct RTL generation remains difficult to validate, optimize, and integrate with compiler-based hardware design flows. Hardware compiler infrastructures such as CIRCT provide typed intermediate representations, legality checks, and optimization passes, yet current LLMs struggle to emit raw compiler IR because of MLIR syntax, SSA discipline, dialect-specific operations, and strict width constraints. This paper presents CPPL, a compiler-mediated design framework that turns LLM-assisted hardware generation into a statically checkable frontend problem rather than an unconstrained RTL text-generation task. CPPL combines a Python frontend DSL for declaring module interfaces and hierarchy with CPPL IR, a JSON-based circuit IR designed to expose compiler-visible structure while remaining accessible to LLMs. The compiler infers operation widths from declared module ports, validates generated IR, checks hierarchy and port bindings, and deterministically lowers the result to CIRCT for synthesizable Verilog generation. On the RTLLM benchmark, CPPL improves functional correctness over direct Verilog and direct CIRCT IR generation, while CIRCT optimization reduces post-synthesis AIG node counts. These results show that a compiler-mediated interface can make LLM-assisted hardware design more reliable, analyzable, and amenable to backend optimization. CPPL is available at https://github.com/SawyDust1228/CPPL.

</details>


### [335] [Building Reliable Arithmetic Multipliers Under NBTI Aging and Process Variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18444)
*Masoud Heidary,Biresh Kumar Joardar*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用乘法符号不变性的新型硬件老化缓解技术，通过选择性应用二进制补码变换来重新分配晶体管应力，减少NBTI老化效应，并成功集成到脉动阵列中，实验证明能显著延长寿命且开销极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬件老化（特别是NBTI效应）会导致集成电路性能下降乃至失效，而AI工作负载因大量依赖乘法运算会加速乘法器老化，现有缓解技术存在局限性。

Method: 利用乘法的符号不变性，对输入数据选择性应用2的补码变换，重新分配晶体管应力以均衡老化，并将该方法集成到脉动阵列（AI加速器）中。

Result: 使用Cadence工具的实验评估表明，与无缓解的自然老化基线相比，该方法显著延长了乘法器寿命，且面积和延迟开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 提出了一种高效、低开销的NBTI老化缓解技术，适用于AI计算场景，对提高现代计算系统可靠性具有实际价值。

Abstract: Hardware aging poses a significant challenge for integrated circuits (ICs), leading to performance degradation and eventual failure. In this work, we focus on the aging of arithmetic multipliers, which are a cornerstone of modern computing systems including in CPUs, GPUs, and FPGAs, as well as AI accelerators like systolic arrays. In particular, AI workloads, which rely predominantly on multiplications, can accelerate Negative Bias Temperature Instability (NBTI) effects in multipliers. This paper presents a novel aging mitigation technique that leverages the signinvariance property of multiplication. By selectively applying 2s complement transformations to inputs, the method redistributes stress across transistors, reducing the effects of NBTI aging. The proposed method is also integrated into systolic arrays, a common AI accelerator, to demonstrate its efficiency in a high-throughput AI accelerator. Experimental evaluations using Cadence tools show better lifetime compared to natural aging (with no mitigation) baseline, while introducing negligible area and delay overheads.

</details>


### [336] [Predictive Software Scheduling as an Early-Warning Hint Layer for Optical Engine Thermal Drift in Heterogeneous SoIC Packaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18612)
*Chi Fei Chung*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 随着半导体工艺进入A16/2nm节点，台积电COUPE架构中的共封装光学集成面临微环谐振器对温度极其敏感的问题，仅±1.7nm的谐振波长漂移就会导致可测量的误码率退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决先进节点下共封装光学集成中热-光耦合带来的性能退化问题。

Method: 基于TSMC COUPE架构，研究PIC层中微环谐振器的温度敏感性对谐振波长和误码率的影响。

Result: 微环谐振器对温度极为敏感，±1.7nm的谐振波长偏差即可导致BER明显退化。

Conclusion: 在A16/2nm先进节点下，热-光耦合问题是CPO集成中不可忽视的关键挑战，需要有效的热管理方案。

Abstract: As semiconductor scaling reaches the A16 / 2 nm node, the integration of co-packaged optics (CPO) via TSMC's Co-Packaged Optics Ultra Engine (COUPE) architecture introduces critical thermal-optical coupling challenges. Micro-ring resonators embedded in the Photonic Integrated Circuit (PIC) layer are exquisitely sensitive to temperature: a deviation of merely +-1.7 nm in resonant wavelength causes measurable Bit Error Rate (BER) degradation.

</details>
